## 2026-07-10 - Remediation Task 1.3

- Request: execute Task 1.3 from `docs/superpowers/plans/2026-07-10-devboard-operational-hardening-remediation.md`.
- Intended write paths: `backend/app/Assistants/ProviderHostResolver.php`, `backend/app/Assistants/SystemProviderHostResolver.php`, `backend/app/Assistants/ProviderEndpointResolution.php`, `backend/tests/Unit/ProviderEndpointPolicyTest.php`, `backend/app/Assistants/ProviderEndpointPolicy.php`, `backend/app/Rules/ProviderEndpointRule.php`, `backend/app/Providers/AppServiceProvider.php`, `backend/tests/Feature/Dashboard/AiAgentRegistryDashboardTest.php`, `backend/config/services.php`, `ai-sandbox/logbooks/LOGBOOK_PROJECT.md`.
- RED verification: `docker exec devboard-app-1 sh -lc 'APP_ENV=testing DB_CONNECTION=sqlite DB_DATABASE=:memory: DB_URL= php artisan test tests/Unit/ProviderEndpointPolicyTest.php tests/Feature/Dashboard/AiAgentRegistryDashboardTest.php --display-warnings'` -> 22 failed, 27 passed (224 assertions). All 20 unit tests failed with `Call to undefined method App\Assistants\ProviderEndpointPolicy::resolve()` (the policy was static/boolean-only and did not resolve DNS or validate individual addresses). Feature test `rejects a provider base URL whose host resolves to a private address before any HTTP request` failed: `Expected response status code [422] but received 200` (the static policy never inspected resolved addresses). Feature test `rejects a stored unsafe provider base URL at model discovery without making an HTTP request` failed: `Failed asserting two strings are identical` — expected `Provider endpoint URL is not allowed.` but got `Could not reach the models endpoint.` (the unsafe URL reached HTTP instead of being rejected pre-flight).
- Work performed: Created `ProviderHostResolver` interface (`resolve(string $host): array` returning normalized A/AAAA addresses). Created `SystemProviderHostResolver` using `dns_get_record($host, DNS_A)` and `DNS_AAAA`; exceptions and non-array results treated as zero answers. Created `ProviderEndpointResolution` readonly value object carrying original hostname, port, scheme, validated addresses, allowed flag, and denial reason. Replaced the static boolean-only `ProviderEndpointPolicy` with an injected policy (constructor takes `ProviderHostResolver`) whose `resolve()` returns `ProviderEndpointResolution`: it parses the absolute URL, requires a host, rejects URL userinfo (`user`/`pass`), keeps the existing development-only (local/testing) HTTP allowance without inferring a new allowlist, strips IPv6 brackets, validates host format (IP literal or dotted DNS name), resolves both A and AAAA via the injected resolver, treats resolver exceptions and zero answers as denied, normalizes IPv4-mapped IPv6 (`::ffff:x.x.x.x` -> IPv4) before range checks, and rejects the entire host if ANY returned address is non-public. Public-ness is enforced with `FILTER_FLAG_NO_PRIV_RANGE | FILTER_FLAG_NO_RES_RANGE` plus explicit checks for IPv4 loopback/unspecified/link-local/multicast and IPv6 `::1`/`::`/`fc00::/7`/`fe80::/10`/`ff00::/8`. A back-compat static `validate()`/`errorMessage()` shim delegates to the container-resolved policy so existing static callers (`AiAgentRegistry`, the validation rule) keep working without modification (out of this task's file list; `AiAgentRegistry.php` is owned by Task 1.4). `ProviderEndpointRule` now resolves the injected policy and uses the resolution's `allowed()` flag; the error message was updated to mention that unresolved hosts are not allowed. Bound `ProviderHostResolver` and `ProviderEndpointPolicy` as singletons in `AppServiceProvider` (system resolver is the default; tests bind fakes). All feature tests bind a deterministic fake resolver in `beforeEach` (returns a public IP by default) so no live DNS is used. Two new dashboard feature tests prove unsafe URLs are rejected before any HTTP request via `Http::preventStrayRequests()`: a hostname resolving to a private IP is rejected with a 422 at store time, and a stored unsafe URL is rejected at model discovery returning `Provider endpoint URL is not allowed.` without making an HTTP call. ## 2026-07-10 - Remediation Task 1.1

- Request: execute Task 1.1 from `docs/superpowers/plans/2026-07-10-devboard-operational-hardening-remediation.md`.
- Intended write paths: `backend/app/Services/ArtifactStorageService.php`, `backend/app/Http/Controllers/Plugin/GenesisChunkController.php`, `backend/app/Http/Controllers/Plugin/DeltaChunkController.php`, `backend/app/Http/Controllers/Plugin/GenesisFinalizeController.php`, `backend/app/Http/Controllers/Plugin/DeltaFinalizeController.php`, `backend/app/Services/GenesisFinalizeService.php`, `backend/app/Services/DeltaFinalizeService.php`, `backend/tests/Feature/GenesisUploadTest.php`, `backend/tests/Feature/DeltaSyncTest.php`, `backend/tests/Feature/Plugin/ArtifactUploadLimitsTest.php`, `docs/ai-devboard/04_PLUGIN_SERVER_CONTRACT.md`, `docs/ai-devboard/05_GENESIS_IMPORT.md`, `docs/ai-devboard/06_DELTA_SYNC.md`, `ai-sandbox/logbooks/LOGBOOK_PROJECT.md`.
- RED verification: `docker exec devboard-app-1 sh -lc 'APP_ENV=testing DB_CONNECTION=sqlite DB_DATABASE=:memory: DB_URL= php artisan test tests/Feature/Plugin/ArtifactUploadLimitsTest.php tests/Feature/GenesisUploadTest.php tests/Feature/DeltaSyncTest.php --display-warnings'` -> 13 failed, 34 passed (255 assertions). Every new test failed with `Expected response status code [422] but received 200`: the range tests (-1, ==chunk_count, 999) created a chunk file and returned 200; the chunk size-mismatch tests (declared size 5, chunk 1 = `def` 3 bytes -> 6 > 5) returned 200 instead of 422; the finalize size-mismatch tests (declared size 10, content `hello` 5 bytes whose SHA matches the manifest) reached SHA validation (which passed) instead of size validation and finalized successfully with status 200.
- Work performed: TDD flow. `ArtifactStorageService::storeChunk()` now reloads the artifact row inside `DB::transaction()` with `lockForUpdate()`, decodes `metadata` with `JSON_THROW_ON_ERROR`, rejects `chunkIndex < 0 || chunkIndex >= chunk_count` with `artifact_chunk_out_of_range` before building a path, rechecks `max_chunk_bytes` as defense in depth, sums existing expected chunk sizes for indexes `0..chunk_count-1` (via `$disk->size()`, no directory scan), and rejects `existing + incoming > size_bytes` with `artifact_size_mismatch` before writing. Same-index/same-hash idempotency preserved (equal hash returns existing path; different hash throws `artifact_finalize_conflict`). `assembleArtifact()` now tracks `$actualSize` while streaming, throws `artifact_size_mismatch` as soon as bytes exceed the declaration and again if the final size is not exactly equal, keeps SHA validation as a separate check after exact-size validation, and deletes the partial output on every assembly failure. Genesis/Delta chunk controllers now accept `string $chunk`, validate it explicitly with `filter_var(FILTER_VALIDATE_INT)` rejecting non-integer, negative, and overflow values with `artifact_chunk_out_of_range` (422) before any storage call, and map both new errors (`artifact_chunk_out_of_range`, `artifact_size_mismatch`) to HTTP 422 via a `mapStatus()` helper (default 409 for conflict/hash mismatch). Genesis/Delta finalize controllers map both new errors to 422. Genesis/Delta finalize services lock artifact rows with `lockForUpdate()` ordered by `id` before assembly so chunk writes and finalization cannot race. Documented both error codes and exact-size semantics in `04_PLUGIN_SERVER_CONTRACT.md`, `05_GENESIS_IMPORT.md`, and `06_DELTA_SYNC.md`.
- GREEN verification: `docker exec devboard-app-1 sh -lc 'APP_ENV=testing DB_CONNECTION=sqlite DB_DATABASE=:memory: DB_URL= php artisan test tests/Feature/Plugin/ArtifactIdentityValidationTest.php tests/Feature/Plugin/ArtifactUploadLimitsTest.php tests/Feature/GenesisUploadTest.php tests/Feature/DeltaSyncTest.php --display-warnings'` -> 60 passed (312 assertions); broader regression (PluginAuthTest, GenesisGraphImportTest, DomainSchemaTest) -> 93 passed (476 assertions); `./vendor/bin/phpstan analyse --configuration=phpstan.neon.dist --no-progress` -> `[OK] No errors`; `git diff --check` -> `DIFFCHECK_OK`.
- Files changed: `backend/app/Services/ArtifactStorageService.php`, `backend/app/Http/Controllers/Plugin/GenesisChunkController.php`, `backend/app/Http/Controllers/Plugin/DeltaChunkController.php`, `backend/app/Http/Controllers/Plugin/GenesisFinalizeController.php`, `backend/app/Http/Controllers/Plugin/DeltaFinalizeController.php`, `backend/app/Services/GenesisFinalizeService.php`, `backend/app/Services/DeltaFinalizeService.php`, `backend/tests/Feature/GenesisUploadTest.php`, `backend/tests/Feature/DeltaSyncTest.php`, `backend/tests/Feature/Plugin/ArtifactUploadLimitsTest.php`, `docs/ai-devboard/04_PLUGIN_SERVER_CONTRACT.md`, `docs/ai-devboard/05_GENESIS_IMPORT.md`, `docs/ai-devboard/06_DELTA_SYNC.md`, `ai-sandbox/logbooks/LOGBOOK_PROJECT.md`.
- Residual risks: none. Concurrency between finalize (locks all artifact rows by id) and a chunk write (locks a single artifact row) is serialized by `lockForUpdate`; real concurrent load was not exercised under SQLite, but the lock ordering is deterministic (single-row chunk writers vs. ordered-by-id finalize) which avoids classic ABAB deadlock. The `size_bytes` exact-size budget is enforced at chunk-upload time and re-verified at assembly time (defense in depth); a client that declares the exact `size_bytes` but uploads fewer chunks still triggers `artifact_chunk_missing` at finalize, and a surplus triggers `artifact_size_mismatch`.

Created failing limit tests (`ArtifactUploadLimitsTest.php`) with 4 tests: rejects oversize size_bytes, rejects excess chunk_count, rejects oversize chunk body (413), and assembles two chunks using streaming without PHP string concatenation. Enforced manifest limits via `max:` validation rules in Genesis/Delta start controllers. Enforced chunk size limit (413 with `artifact_chunk_too_large`) in Genesis/Delta chunk controllers. Replaced string concatenation in `ArtifactStorageService::assembleArtifact()` with `hash_init/hash_update/hash_final` and `fopen/fwrite` to temp file path on configured disk. Updated `artifacts.py` to read files with `open("rb")` in chunked loops instead of `read_bytes()` for both genesis and delta uploads. Updated plugin test to verify chunked reading. Verified all backend and plugin tests pass.

- Residual risks: the streaming approach reads one chunk at a time via Storage::get() (max 8MB per read) but does not hold the full artifact in a PHP string variable. Temp file is placed within the configured local disk path. Python chunked reads are bounded by chunk_size (default ~5MB).

## 2026-07-09 - Task 1.4: Bind Plugin Tokens To Signed Device Requests

- Request: execute Task 1.4 from the DevBoard Operational Hardening plan using TDD. Add device signing secret storage, PluginRequestSigner service, enforce HMAC signatures for device-bound tokens in middleware, and update Python plugin to sign requests.
- Context read: `AGENTS.md`, `ai-sandbox/INIT.md`, all existing files listed in the task, existing test suites, `backend/tests/Feature/PluginAuthTest.php`, `backend/app/Http/Controllers/Plugin/RegisterDeviceController.php`, `backend/app/Services/PluginTokenService.php`, `backend/app/Http/Middleware/AuthenticatePluginToken.php`, `plugin/src/devboard_plugin/client.py`, `plugin/src/devboard_plugin/config.py`, `plugin/tests/test_client.py`, `plugin/tests/test_config.py`.
- Intended write paths: `backend/database/migrations/*_add_signing_secret_to_devices.php` (new), `backend/app/Services/PluginRequestSigner.php` (new), `backend/app/Http/Controllers/Plugin/RegisterDeviceController.php`, `backend/app/Services/PluginTokenService.php`, `backend/app/Http/Middleware/AuthenticatePluginToken.php`, `backend/tests/Feature/PluginAuthTest.php`, `plugin/src/devboard_plugin/client.py`, `plugin/src/devboard_plugin/config.py`, `plugin/tests/test_client.py`, `plugin/tests/test_config.py`, `ai-sandbox/logbooks/LOGBOOK_PROJECT.md`.
- Work performed: followed TDD order across all 9 steps. Created `backend/database/migrations/2026_07_09_000004_add_signing_secret_to_devices.php` adding `signing_secret_hash` (nullable, string, 64) to `devices`. Created `backend/app/Services/PluginRequestSigner.php` with canoncial string building, HMAC-SHA256 computation, constant-time comparison, and clock skew validation (300s). Updated `RegisterDeviceController` to generate a one-time 64-char hex secret on new device registration, store `hash('sha256', $plainSecret)` in `signing_secret_hash`, and return `device_secret` in the response. For existing already-active devices, `device_secret` is not returned. Updated `AuthenticatePluginToken` middleware to check for device signature headers after bearer token auth; if device_id is set but no signature headers present, return 401 with `device_signature_required`; if signature is invalid, return 401 with `device_signature_invalid`. Updated Python plugin `DevBoardClient` to sign requests when `device_id` and `device_secret` are present: computes content-sha256 of JSON body, builds canonical string, computes HMAC-SHA256, adds `X-DevBoard-Device-Id`, `X-DevBoard-Timestamp`, `X-DevBoard-Content-SHA256`, and `X-DevBoard-Signature` headers. Updated `Credentials` config dataclass with `device_secret: str | None`. On register device, client stores the returned `device_secret`. Added backend tests: device secret on registration, rejection without signature, stale timestamp rejection, body hash mismatch rejection, and valid signature acceptance. Added Python tests for signature header addition and credentials round-trip.
- Verification: `docker exec devboard-app-1 ... php artisan test tests/Feature/PluginAuthTest.php tests/Feature/Plugin/ArtifactUploadLimitsTest.php tests/Feature/GenesisUploadTest.php tests/Feature/DeltaSyncTest.php tests/Feature/DomainSchemaTest.php --display-warnings` → 37 passed, 255 assertions. `cd plugin && python3 -m pytest -q tests/` → 46 passed. Full backend suite → 411 passed / 3 failed (unrelated pre-existing dashboard test failures: KanbanTaskCreateEditApiTest, ProjectCrudDashboardApiTest, ProjectLifecycleDashboardApiTest).
- Files changed: `backend/database/migrations/2026_07_09_000004_add_signing_secret_to_devices.php` (new), `backend/app/Services/PluginRequestSigner.php` (new), `backend/app/Http/Controllers/Plugin/RegisterDeviceController.php`, `backend/app/Http/Middleware/AuthenticatePluginToken.php`, `backend/tests/Feature/PluginAuthTest.php`, `plugin/src/devboard_plugin/client.py`, `plugin/src/devboard_plugin/config.py`, `plugin/tests/test_client.py`, `ai-sandbox/logbooks/LOGBOOK_PROJECT.md`.
- Residual risks: devices created before this change have NULL `signing_secret_hash` and are exempt from signature enforcement. Legacy tests pass because middleware skips signature check when `signing_secret_hash` is NULL. The signing key derivation uses `sha256(plain_secret)` as the HMAC key (matching the stored `signing_secret_hash`), not the raw plain secret.

## 2026-07-09 - Task 3.2: Resolve Python Internal CALLS Edges

- Request: execute Task 3.2 from the DevBoard Operational Hardening plan using TDD. Make the Python AST analyzer resolve CALLS edges to internal symbol IDs instead of always using `external:<name>`.
- Context read: `analyzer/src/devboard_analyzer/code_graph.py`, `analyzer/tests/test_code_graph.py`, `ai-sandbox/logbooks/LOGBOOK_PROJECT.md`.
- Intended write paths: `analyzer/src/devboard_analyzer/code_graph.py`, `analyzer/tests/test_code_graph.py`, `ai-sandbox/logbooks/LOGBOOK_PROJECT.md`.
- Work performed: TDD flow — wrote two failing tests: one asserting `helper()` call from `caller()` resolves to internal `symbol:{path}:helper` (not `external:helper`), and one asserting `json.dumps()` remains external. Created a two-pass symbol resolution in `_PythonGraphExtractor`: Pass 1 uses a `_SymbolCollector` visitor to scan the AST and build a name→symbol_id index mapping both qualified names (e.g., `Service.ok`) and simple names (e.g., `helper`). Pass 2 uses the existing `_PythonGraphExtractor` with the pre-built index — in `visit_Call`, it looks up the called name in the index first; if found, uses the internal symbol ID; if not, falls back to `external:<name>`.
- Verification: `cd /home/ubuntu/dev-sandbox/analyzer && python3 -m pytest -q` → GREEN (21 passed).
- Files changed: `analyzer/src/devboard_analyzer/code_graph.py`, `analyzer/tests/test_code_graph.py`, `ai-sandbox/logbooks/LOGBOOK_PROJECT.md`.
- Residual risks: forward-referenced calls (where the callee is defined after the caller in the source) are correctly resolved because the two-pass approach collects all symbols before any edge generation. Simple-name ambiguity (two symbols with the same simple name but different qualified names) resolves to whichever was collected first — typically the outer-scope definition since AST traversal visits outer scopes first.
